directories: %v\", err)\n192\t\t\treturn metrics, nil\n193\t\t}\n194\t\n195\t\tif len(projectDirs) == 0 {\n196\t\t\tmetrics.Error = \"No Claude projects found\"\n197\t\t\treturn metrics, nil\n198\t\t}\n199\t\n200\t\t// Collect JSONL files from all project directories (recursive — includes subagents)\n201\t\tvar files []string\n202\t\tfor _, projectDir := range projectDirs {\n203\t\t\tdirFiles, err := findJSONLFilesRecursive(projectDir)\n204\t\t\tif err != nil {\n205\t\t\t\tcontinue\n206\t\t\t}\n207\t\t\tfiles = append(files, dirFiles...)\n208\t\t}\n209\t\n210\t\tif len(files) == 0 {\n211\t\t\tmetrics.Error = \"No JSONL files found in any project\"\n212\t\t\treturn metrics, nil\n213\t\t}\n214\t\n215\t\t// Step 1: Ingest any new data from JSONL files into SQLite\n216\t\t// Uses pre-aggregation for complete files to reduce I/O\n217\t\tcompleteThreshold := GetFileCompleteThreshold()\n218\t\tfor _, file := range files {\n219\t\t\tfileInfo, err := os.Stat(file)\n220\t\t\tif err != nil {\n221\t\t\t\tcontinue // File may have been deleted\n222\t\t\t}\n223\t\n224\t\t\t// Check if file is already marked complete and unchanged\n225\t\t\tif agg, ok := tc.cache.GetFileAggregate(file); ok && agg.IsComplete {\n226\t\t\t\tif !fileInfo.ModTime().After(agg.CompletedAt) {\n227\t\t\t\t\t// File is complete and unchanged - skip all file I/O\n228\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n229\t\t\t\t}\n230\t\t\t\t// File was modified after being marked complete - reactivate it\n231\t\t\t\ttc.cache.MarkFileActive(file)\n232\t\t\t}\n233\t\n234\t\t\t// Check if file should be marked complete (hasn't been modified in threshold duration)\n235\t\t\tif time.Since(fileInfo.ModTime()) > completeThreshold {\n236\t\t\t\t// Process any remaining data first\n237\t\t\t\tif err := tc.ingestJSONLFile(file); err == nil {\n238\t\t\t\t\t// Mark as complete and pre-aggregate\n239\t\t\t\t\ttc.cache.MarkFileComplete(file)\n240\t\t\t\t}\n241\t\t\t\tcontinue\n242\t\t\t}\n243\t\n244\t\t\t// Active file - normal incremental processing\n245\t\t\ttc.ingestJSONLFile(file)\n246\t\t}\n247\t\n248\t\t// Step 2: Query SQLite using hybrid approach (pre-aggregated + active events)\n249\t\taggregated, err := tc.cache.QueryTokensHybrid(tc.lookbackFrom)\n250\t\tif err != nil {\n251\t\t\tmetrics.Error = fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to query token cache: %v\", err)\n252\t\t\treturn metrics, nil\n253\t\t}\n254\t\n255\t\t// Populate metrics from query results\n256\t\tmetrics.InputTokens = aggregated.InputTokens\n257\t\tmetrics.OutputTokens = aggregated.OutputTokens\n258\t\tmetrics.CacheReadTokens = aggregated.CacheReadTokens\n259\t\tmetrics.CacheCreationTokens = aggregated.CacheCreationTokens\n260\t\tmetrics.TotalTokens = aggregated.InputTokens + aggregated.OutputTokens +\n261\t\t\taggregated.CacheReadTokens + aggregated.CacheCreationTokens\n262\t\tmetrics.Prompts = aggregated.EventCount\n263\t\tmetrics.EarliestTimestamp = aggregated.EarliestTimestamp\n264\t\tmetrics.LatestTimestamp = aggregated.LatestTimestamp\n265\t\n266\t\tif !aggregated.EarliestTimestamp.IsZero() && !aggregated.LatestTimestamp.IsZero() {\n267\t\t\tmetrics.TimeSpan = aggregated.LatestTimestamp.Sub(aggregated.EarliestTimestamp)\n268\t\t}\n269\t\n270\t\t// Build model list and per-model usage\n271\t\tvar totalCost float64\n272\t\tmetrics.ModelUsages = make([]ModelUsage, 0, len(aggregated.ModelMetrics))\n273\t\n274\t\tfor model, mm := range aggregated.ModelMetrics {\n275\t\t\tmetrics.Models = append(metrics.Models, model)\n276\t\n277\t\t\tpricing := getPricingForModel(model)\n278\t\t\tinputCost := float64(mm.InputTokens) * pricing.InputPerMillion / 1_000_000\n279\t\t\toutputCost := float64(mm.OutputTokens) * pricing.OutputPerMillion / 1_000_000\n280\t\t\tcacheReadCost := float64(mm.CacheReadTokens) * pricing.CacheReadPerMillion / 1_000_000\n281\t\t\tcacheCreateCost := float64(mm.CacheCreationTokens) * pricing.CacheCreatePerMillion / 1_000_000\n282\t\t\tmodelCost := inputCost + outputCost + cacheReadCost + cacheCreateCost\n283\t\n284\t\t\tusage := ModelUsage{\n285\t\t\t\tModel:               model,\n286\t\t\t\tInputTokens:         mm.InputTokens,\n287\t\t\t\tOutputTokens:        mm.OutputTokens,\n288\t\t\t\tCacheReadTokens:     mm.CacheReadTokens,\n289\t\t\t\tCacheCreationTokens: mm.CacheCreationTokens,\n290\t\t\t\tTotalTokens:         mm.InputTokens + mm.OutputTokens + mm.CacheReadTokens + mm.CacheCreationTokens,\n291\t\t\t\tCost:                modelCost,\n292\t\t\t}\n293\t\t\tmetrics.ModelUsages = append(metrics.ModelUsages, usage)\n294\t\t\ttotalCost += modelCost\n295\t\t}\n296\t\n297\t\tsort.Strings(metrics.Models)\n298\t\n299\t\t// Sort model usages by cost (highest first)\n300\t\tsort.Slice(metrics.ModelUsages, func(i, j int) bool {\n301\t\t\treturn metrics.ModelUsages[i].Cost > metrics.ModelUsages[j].Cost\n302\t\t})\n303\t\n304\t\tmetrics.TotalCost = totalCost\n305\t\n306\t\t// Calculate session average rate\n307\t\tif metrics.TimeSpan > 0 {\n308\t\t\tminutes := metrics.TimeSpan.Minutes()\n309\t\t\tif minutes > 0 {\n310\t\t\t\tmetrics.SessionAvgRate = float64(metrics.TotalTokens) / minutes\n311\t\t\t}\n312\t\t}\n313\t\n314\t\t// Calculate 60-second window rate from recent events\n315\t\trecentEvents, err := tc.cache.QueryRecentEvents(60)\n316\t\tif err == nil && len(recentEvents) > 0 {\n317\t\t\tmetrics.Rate = tc.calculate60sRate(recentEvents)\n318\t\t}\n319\t\n320\t\tmetrics.Available = true\n321\t\treturn metrics, nil\n322\t}\n323\t\n324\t// ingestJSONLFile reads a JSONL file and inserts new events into SQLite\n325\t// Returns an error if database operations fail (for proper error handling)\n326\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) ingestJSONLFile(filename string) error {\n327\t\tif tc.cache == nil {\n328\t\t\treturn nil\n329\t\t}\n330\t\n331\t\t// Check file modification time\n332\t\tfileInfo, err := os.Stat(filename)\n333\t\tif err != nil {\n334\t\t\treturn nil // File may have been deleted, not a critical error\n335\t\t}\n336\t\n337\t\t// Get last processed state\n338\t\tlastLine, lastMod, exists := tc.cache.GetFileState(filename)\n339\t\n340\t\t// If file hasn't been modified since last processing, skip\n341\t\tif exists && !fileInfo.ModTime().After(lastMod) {\n342\t\t\treturn nil\n343\t\t}\n344\t\n345\t\t// If file was modified (truncated/rewritten), invalidate and reprocess\n346\t\tif exists && fileInfo.ModTime().After(lastMod) {\n347\t\t\t// Check if file was truncated (new size < last line count implies rewrite)\n348\t\t\t// For safety, we'll just process from where we left off\n349\t\t\t// but if file was completely rewritten, invalidate\n350\t\t\tfile, err := os.Open(filename)\n351\t\t\tif err != nil {\n352\t\t\t\treturn nil // File may have been deleted\n353\t\t\t}\n354\t\t\tdefer file.Close()\n355\t\n356\t\t\t// Count current lines\n357\t\t\tvar currentLineCount int64\n358\t\t\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(file)\n359\t\t\tbuf := make([]byte, 0, 1024*1024)\n360\t\t\tscanner.Buffer(buf, 10*1024*1024)\n361\t\t\tfor scanner.Scan() {\n362\t\t\t\tcurrentLineCount++\n363\t\t\t}\n364\t\n365\t\t\t// If file has fewer lines than we processed, it was rewritten\n366\t\t\tif currentLineCount < lastLine {\n367\t\t\t\tif err := tc.cache.InvalidateFile(filename); err != nil {\n368\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to invalidate file %s: %w\", filename, err)\n369\t\t\t\t}\n370\t\t\t\tlastLine = 0\n371\t\t\t}\n372\t\t}\n373\t\n374\t\t// Open file for processing\n375\t\tfile, err := os.Open(filename)\n376\t\tif err != nil {\n377\t\t\treturn nil // File may have been deleted\n378\t\t}\n379\t\tdefer file.Close()\n380\t\n381\t\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(file)\n382\t\tbuf := make([]byte, 0, 1024*1024)\n383\t\tscanner.Buffer(buf, 10*1024*1024)\n384\t\n385\t\tvar lineNumber int64\n386\t\tvar events []TokenEvent\n387\t\n388\t\tfor scanner.Scan() {\n389\t\t\tlineNumber++\n390\t\n391\t\t\t// Skip already processed lines\n392\t\t\tif lineNumber <= lastLine {\n393\t\t\t\tcontinue\n394\t\t\t}\n395\t\n396\t\t\tvar msg claudeMessage\n397\t\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal(scanner.Bytes(), &msg); err != nil {\n398\t\t\t\tcontinue\n399\t\t\t}\n400\t\n401\t\t\t// Only process assistant messages (count all requests, even with zero tokens)\n402\t\t\tif msg.Type != \"assistant\" {\n403\t\t\t\tcontinue\n404\t\t\t}\n405\t\n406\t\t\t// Parse timestamp\n407\t\t\ttimestamp, err := time.Parse(time.RFC3339Nano, msg.Timestamp)\n408\t\t\tif err != nil {\n409\t\t\t\tcontinue\n410\t\t\t}\n411\t\n412\t\t\tusage := msg.Message.Usage\n413\t\t\tcacheCreation := usage.CacheCreationInputTokens\n414\t\t\tif cacheCreation == 0 {\n415\t\t\t\tcacheCreation = usage.CacheCreation.Ephemeral5mInputTokens +\n416\t\t\t\t\tusage.CacheCreation.Ephemeral1hInputTokens\n417\t\t\t}\n418\t\n419\t\t\tevents = append(events, TokenEvent{\n420\t\t\t\tTimestamp:           timestamp,\n421\t\t\t\tModel:               msg.Message.Model,\n422\t\t\t\tInputTokens:         usage.InputTokens,\n423\t\t\t\tOutputTokens:        usage.OutputTokens,\n424\t\t\t\tCacheReadTokens:     usage.CacheReadInputTokens,\n425\t\t\t\tCacheCreationTokens: cacheCreation,\n426\t\t\t\tSourceFile:          filename,\n427\t\t\t\tLineNumber:          lineNumber,\n428\t\t\t})\n429\t\n430\t\t\t// Batch insert every 100 events\n431\t\t\tif len(events) >= 100 {\n432\t\t\t\tif err := tc.cache.InsertTokenEventBatch(events); err != nil {\n433\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to insert batch for %s: %w\", filename, err)\n434\t\t\t\t}\n435\t\t\t\tevents = events[:0]\n436\t\t\t}\n437\t\t}\n438\t\n439\t\t// Insert remaining events\n440\t\tif len(events) > 0 {\n441\t\t\tif err := tc.cache.InsertTokenEventBatch(events); err != nil {\n442\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to insert final batch for %s: %w\", filename, err)\n443\t\t\t}\n444\t\t}\n445\t\n446\t\t// Update file state\n447\t\tif err := tc.cache.SetFileState(filename, lineNumber, fileInfo.ModTime()); err != nil {\n448\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to set file state for %s: %w\", filename, err)\n449\t\t}\n450\t\n451\t\treturn nil\n452\t}\n453\t\n454\t// findProjectDir finds the Claude project directory for the given working directory,\n455\t// searching across all configured roots.\n456\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) findProjectDir(cwd string) string {\n457\t\tprojectName := strings.ReplaceAll(cwd, \"/\", \"-\")\n458\t\tfor _, root := range tc.projectsDirs {\n459\t\t\tprojectPath := filepath.Join(root, projectName)\n460\t\t\tif _, err := os.Stat(projectPath); err == nil {\n461\t\t\t\treturn projectPath\n462\t\t\t}\n463\t\t}\n464\t\treturn \"\"\n465\t}\n466\t\n467\t// findAllProjectDirs returns all project directories found under all configured roots.\n468\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) findAllProjectDirs() ([]string, error) {\n469\t\tvar dirs []string\n470\t\tfor _, root := range tc.projectsDirs {\n471\t\t\tif root == \"\" {\n472\t\t\t\tcontinue\n473\t\t\t}\n474\t\t\tif _, err := os.Stat(root); os.IsNotExist(err) {\n475\t\t\t\tcontinue\n476\t\t\t}\n477\t\t\tentries, err := os.ReadDir(root)\n478\t\t\tif err != nil {\n479\t\t\t\tcontinue\n480\t\t\t}\n481\t\t\tfor _, entry := range entries {\n482\t\t\t\tif entry.IsDir() {\n483\t\t\t\t\tdirs = append(dirs, filepath.Join(root, entry.Name()))\n484\t\t\t\t}\n485\t\t\t}\n486\t\t}\n487\t\treturn dirs, nil\n488\t}\n489\t\n490\t// findJSONLFilesRecursive returns all *.jsonl files under dir, including subdirectories.\n491\t// This captures subagent files stored at <project>/<uuid>/subagents/agent-*.jsonl\n492\t// in addition to the top-level <project>/<uuid>.jsonl conversation files.\n493\tfunc findJSONLFilesRecursive(dir string) ([]string, error) {\n494\t\tvar files []string\n495\t\terr := filepath.Walk(dir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {\n496\t\t\tif err != nil {\n497\t\t\t\treturn nil\n498\t\t\t}\n499\t\t\tif !info.IsDir() && strings.HasSuffix(path, \".jsonl\") {\n500\t\t\t\tfiles = append(files, path)\n501\t\t\t}\n502\t\t\treturn nil\n503\t\t})\n504\t\treturn files, err\n505\t}\n506\t\n507\t// calculate60sRate calculates the token rate over the last 60 seconds\n508\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) calculate60sRate(events []TimestampedTokens) float64 {\n509\t\tif len(events) == 0 {\n510\t\t\treturn 0\n511\t\t}\n512\t\n513\t\t// Get the most recent timestamp\n514\t\tlastTime := events[len(events)-1].Timestamp\n515\t\tcutoffTime := lastTime.Add(-60 * time.Second)\n516\t\n517\t\t// Sum tokens in the last 60 seconds\n518\t\tvar totalTokens int64\n519\t\tvar windowStart time.Time\n520\t\n521\t\tfor i := len(events) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n522\t\t\tif events[i].Timestamp.Before(cutoffTime) {\n523\t\t\t\tbreak\n524\t\t\t}\n525\t\t\ttotalTokens += events[i].Tokens\n526\t\t\twindowStart = events[i].Timestamp\n527\t\t}\n528\t\n529\t\t// Calculate rate (tokens per minute)\n530\t\tif totalTokens == 0 {\n531\t\t\treturn 0\n532\t\t}\n533\t\n534\t\tduration := lastTime.Sub(windowStart)\n535\t\tif duration <= 0 {\n536\t\t\treturn 0\n537\t\t}\n538\t\n539\t\tminutes := duration.Minutes()\n540\t\tif minutes == 0 {\n541\t\t\treturn 0\n542\t\t}\n543\t\n544\t\treturn float64(totalTokens) / minutes\n545\t}\n546\t\n547\t// ModelPricing contains pricing rates for a Claude model\n548\ttype ModelPricing struct time.Now()\n\t// Find the most recent Monday\n\tweekday := int(now.Weekday())\n\tif weekday == 0 {\n\t\tweekday = 7 // Sunday becomes 7 for easier math\n\t}\n\tdaysUntilMonday := weekday - 1 // Days since Monday (Mon=0, Tue=1, ...)\n\n\t// Start of Monday (midnight)\n\tmonday := now.AddDate(0, 0, -daysUntilMonday)\n\tmonday = time.Date(monday.Year(), monday.Month(), monday.Day(), 9, 0, 0, 0, monday.Location())\n\n\t// If we haven't reached 9am on Monday yet, go back to previous Monday\n\tif monday.After(now) {\n\t\tmonday = monday.AddDate(0, 0, -7)\n\t}\n\n\treturn monday\n}\n\n// timestamp\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) Collect() (*TokenMetrics, error) {\n\tmetrics := &TokenMetrics{\n\t\tAvailable:    false,\n\t\tLastUpdate:   time.Now(),\n\t\tLookbackFrom: model)\n\n\t\tpricing := getPricingForModel(model)\n\t\tinputCost := float64(mm.InputTokens) * pricing.InputPerMillion / 1_000_000\n\t\toutputCost := float64(mm.OutputTokens) * pricing.OutputPerMillion / 1_000_000\n\t\tcacheReadCost := float64(mm.CacheReadTokens) * pricing.CacheReadPerMillion / 1_000_000\n\t\tcacheCreateCost := float64(mm.CacheCreationTokens) * pricing.CacheCreatePerMillion / 1_000_000\n\t\tmodelCost := inputCost + outputCost + cacheReadCost + cacheCreateCost\n\n\t\tusage := ModelUsage{\n\t\t\tModel:               model,\n\t\t\tInputTokens:         mm.InputTokens,\n\t\t\tOutputTokens:        mm.OutputTokens,\n\t\t\tCacheReadTokens:     mm.CacheReadTokens,\n\t\t\tCacheCreationTokens: mm.CacheCreationTokens,\n\t\t\tTotalTokens:         mm.InputTokens + mm.OutputTokens + mm.CacheReadTokens + mm.CacheCreationTokens,\n\t\t\tCost:                modelCost,\n\t\t}\n\t\tmetrics.ModelUsages = append(metrics.ModelUsages, usage)\n\t\ttotalCost += modelCost\n\t}\n\n\tsort.Strings(metrics.Models)\n\n\t// Sort model usages by cost (highest first)\n\tsort.Slice(metrics.ModelUsages, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\treturn metrics.ModelUsages[i].Cost > metrics.ModelUsages[j].Cost\n\t})\n\n\tmetrics.TotalCost = totalCost\n\n\t// Calculate session average rate\n\tif metrics.TimeSpan > 0 {\n\t\tminutes := metrics.TimeSpan.Minutes()\n\t\tif minutes > 0 {\n\t\t\tmetrics.SessionAvgRate = float64(metrics.TotalTokens) / minutes\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Calculate 60-second window rate from recent
